# -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
# Ion codes
#
# The following codes use the PDG-2006 conventions. 
# The (hyper)nuclear codes are given as a 10-digit number: 10LZZZAAAI where 
#   - AAA is the total baryon number, 
#   - ZZZ is the total charge,
#   - L is the number of strange quarks,
#   - I is the isomer number (I=0 corresponds to the ground state)
# See the Particle Data book for more details
# -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#
# Jul, 2014 Zr, Nb, Hf, Os, Zr, Bi nuclei were added (N. Geary and S. Dytman) 
#    get atomic mass from Wikipedia, e.g. "isotopes of hafnium"
#    convert to GeV with .9314941 GeV/c^2/amu
#    subtract .000510998928 GeV per electron
#    this is nuclear mass, looks like most of the existing entries are atomic mass
#
#---------
# Rare Earth Elements
# http://nuclear.calpoly.edu/~niffte/viewvc.cgi/trunk/common/utils/?root=NIFFTE
# modified version of ripl2pdg.C
